debug_decisions = {
	TUR_reload_minority_values = {
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		complete_effect = { ottoman_minority_variable_check = yes }
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
	TUR_bop_right = {
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		complete_effect = {
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = TUR_unionist_struggle
				value = 2
			}
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = TUR_local_central_rule
				value = 2
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
	TUR_bop_left = {
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		complete_effect = {
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = TUR_unionist_struggle
				value = -2
			}
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = TUR_local_central_rule
				value = -2
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
	TUR_spawn_ottoman_syria = {
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		complete_effect = {
			complete_national_focus = TUR_three_pasha_government
			complete_national_focus = TUR_assign_cemal_to_syria
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 0 }
	}
}

GER_great_war = {
	TUR_surrender_to_entente = {
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		fire_only_once = yes
		activation = {
			has_capitulated = no
			is_in_faction = yes
			is_faction_leader = no
			is_subject = no
			has_war_with = FRA
			FRA = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { has_country_flag = great_war_loser }
			}
			has_global_flag = great_war
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = great_war_loser
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				has_global_flag = GER_capitulation
				has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation
			}
			surrender_progress > 0.2
			OR = {
				surrender_progress > 0.4
				# war is losing
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_capitulated = yes
				}
				faction_leader = {
					surrender_progress > 0.1
				}
				# so fucked
				has_war_support < 0.2
				has_stability < 0.2
				# Constantinople lost
				NOT = { controls_state = 347 }
				# Constantinople threatened
				any_enemy_country = {
					OR = {
						controls_state = 341
						controls_state = 347
						controls_state = 756
						controls_state = 825
						controls_state = 860
					}
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			controls_state = 347
			surrender_progress < 0.4
			has_war_support > 0.2
			has_stability > 0.2
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_capitulated = yes
				has_war = no
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
				has_global_flag = GER_capitulation
				has_global_flag = FRA_capitulation
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = no
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		timeout_effect = {
			add_ideas = TUR_mudros_armistice
			if = {
				limit = { has_war_with = ENG }
				ENG = { country_event = { id = ww1_england.264 hours = 3 } }
			}
			else = { FRA = { country_event = { id = ww1_england.264 hours = 3 } } }
			hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = ww1_england.265 hours = 10 } }
		}
	}

					OR = {

							is_core_of = EGY
						}
					}
					add_resistance = 15
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = TUR_jihad_declared

			add_to_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_morale_factor = 0.03 }
			set_variable = { TUR_aoabe_weekly_casualties_war_support = 0.002 }
		}

			base = 1000
		}

	TUR_invoke_senussiya_alliance = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_nationalism
		allowed = {
			original_tag = TUR
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = great_war
			is_subject = no
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			}
			FROM = {
				is_subject = no
				is_in_faction = no
				OR = {
					has_government = neutrality
					has_government = fascism
				}	
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = TUR
					has_war_together_with = TUR
					has_country_flag = LBA_modus_vivendi_of_acroma
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					LBA = {
						is_ai = no
					}
				}
				is_in_faction = yes
			}	
		}
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = LBA
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_war = yes
			any_country = {
				has_war_with = TUR
				any_owned_state = {
					is_core_of = LBA
				}
			}
		}
		days_remove = 14
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					LBA = {
						is_ai = yes				
					}
				}				
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = TUR
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = LBA
						}
					}
					LBA = {
						add_to_war = {
							targeted_alliance = TUR
							enemy = PREV
						}	
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction = yes	
					}
					add_to_faction = LBA
				}
				else = {
					LBA = {
						country_event = generic.5
					}
				}
			}	
			LBA = {
				set_country_flag = TUR_invoke_senussiya_alliance
			}	
		}
		cost = 15
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = ITA
				factor = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				date < 1915.11.1
				factor = 0
			}

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_fundraising
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		cost = 10
		state_target = yes
		targets = { 847 }
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				OR = {
					state = 847
					state = 106
					state = 848
					state = 760
					state = 761
				}
				is_controlled_by = TUR
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		on_map_mode = map_only
		days_remove = 35
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = TUR_increase_taxes_on_albanians
			NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_increase_taxes_on_albanians_kosova }
			OR = {
				controls_state = 847
				controls_state = 106
				controls_state = 848
				controls_state = 760
				controls_state = 761
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = TUR_kosova }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_tax_collection days = 365 }
				set_state_flag = TUR_albanian_tax_resistance
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_albanian_tax_resistance }
					custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_tax_collection_in_albania_tt2
					add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_resistance_target = 0.2 }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_increase_kosova_centralization_10
			add_to_variable = { global.TUR_kosova_centralization = 0.1 }
			set_country_flag = TUR_increase_taxes_on_albanians_kosova
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ottoman.106 days = 4 } }
			ottoman_minority_variable_check = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 100 }
	}

		icon = GFX_decision_infiltrate_state
		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }

			870

			871
			803

			758
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = TUR_centralize_albania
			controls_state = FROM
			FROM = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_state_level > 0 } }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					FROM = {
						OR = {
							state = 847
							state = 106
							state = 848
							state = 760
							state = 761
						}
					}
					check_variable = { global.TUR_kosova_centralization < 0.8 }
				}
				AND = {
					FROM = {
						OR = {
							state = 758
							state = 803
							state = 871
						}
					}
					check_variable = { global.TUR_yanya_centralization < 0.85 }
				}
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						state = 870
						state = 44
					}
					check_variable = { global.TUR_iskodra_centralization < 0.85 }
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_albania_centralization_level = 0 } }
					resistance < 50
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_albania_centralization_level = 1 } }
					resistance < 40
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_albania_centralization_level = 2 } }
					resistance < 30
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_albania_centralization_level = 3 } }
					resistance < 20
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_albania_centralization_level = 4 } }
					resistance < 10
				}
				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_vilayet }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_semi_autonomous_vilayet }
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_centralize_albania_decision_tt
				add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_resistance_target_albanian = 0.2 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = TUR_ottoman_albania_centralization_level }
					add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_albania_centralization_level = 1 }
				}
				else = { set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_albania_centralization_level = 1 } }

							state = 803
							state = 871
						}
					}
				}

				add_to_variable = { global.TUR_yanya_centralization = 0.02 }
			}

peace_deals = {
	TUR_sue_for_peace_ITA = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		allowed = { tag = TUR }
		target_trigger = { FROM = { tag = ITA } }
		available = {
			has_war_with = ITA
			OR = {
				is_in_faction = no
				ITA = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = kis_firstbalkan_war
					has_war_with = BUL
					has_war_with = SER
					has_war_with = GRE
					any_enemy_country = {
						is_major = yes
						NOT = { original_tag = ITA }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = italo_turkish_war
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ITA_libyan_war_mission_timeout
				has_global_flag = italo_turkish_war_ends
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = great_war }
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = great_war_ends
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = FRA
						is_in_faction_with = GER
						has_war_with = FRA
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
			owns_state = 448
			owns_state = 450
			owns_state = 661
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			ITA = { country_event = { id = ww1_italianturkish.4 } }
			TUR_decrease_ittihadist_loyalty = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_war_with = ITA
				OR = {
					casualties > 50000
					ITA = {
						has_full_control_of_state = 448
						has_full_control_of_state = 450
						has_full_control_of_state = 661
						has_full_control_of_state = 663
					}
					AND = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_controlled_by = ITA
							OR = {
								region = 25
								region = 129
								region = 202
							}
						}
						OR = {
							ITA = { controls_state = 448 }
							ITA = { controls_state = 450 }
						}
					}
					surrender_progress > 0.10
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 500
				OR = {
					has_war_with = BUL
					has_war_with = SER
					has_war_with = GRE
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ITA = {
							surrender_progress < 0.05
						}
						NOT = {
							controls_state = 448
							controls_state = 450
						}
					}
					surrender_progress > 0.05
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			ITA = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_italianturkish.4
					hours = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_sue_for_peace_BLL = {

				OR = {

					AND = {

						NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_must_won_bw1 }
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
					}
				}
				OR = {
					#historical trigger
					AND = {
						date < 1913.5.24
						casualties < 350000
						surrender_progress < 0.20
					}
					#dont surrender if you are wining the balkan war
					#ahistorical cases
					SER = {
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = TUR
							has_capitulated = yes
							surrender_progress > 0.3
						}
					}
					BUL = {
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = TUR
							has_capitulated = yes
							surrender_progress > 0.3
						}
					}

							has_capitulated = yes
							surrender_progress > 0.3
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		allowed = { original_tag = TUR }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_arrest_ittihadist
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_CP_30
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 29.99 }

			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TUR_not_ittihadist_power_tt_minimal
				check_variable = { TUR_ittihadist_power > 1 }
			}
		}
		activation = { always = no }

			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -30 }
			TUR_decrease_ittihadist_loyalty = yes
			TUR_decrease_ittihadist_power = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_unit_leader = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_sympathies
							has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_radical_sympathies
						}
					}
				}
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_sympathies
							has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_radical_sympathies
						}
					}
					remove_unit_leader_role = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_command_power = -30
				army_experience = -30
				add_war_support = -0.02
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = TUR_action_army_coup }
				add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = TUR_action_army_coup days = -10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = TUR_raid_on_the_sublime_porte }
				add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = TUR_raid_on_the_sublime_porte days = -10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = TUR_nationalist_retaliation }
				add_days_mission_timeout = { mission = TUR_nationalist_retaliation days = -10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_power_balance = { id = TUR_unionist_struggle } }
				add_power_balance_value = {
					id = TUR_unionist_struggle
					value = 0.1
				}
			}
		}
		days_remove = 35
	}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0

				add = 100

			}
		}
	}

	TRS_dissolve_the_debt_council_decision = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_break_treaty
		allowed = { tag = TUR }
		cost = 150

		available = {

			if = {

				has_completed_focus = TRS_dissolve_the_debt_council
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TUR_OPDA_trigger_tooltip
				has_variable = opda_consumer_goods
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = debt_less_than_0
				check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods < 0 }
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_OPDA_idea }
				remove_ideas = TUR_OPDA_idea
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_OPDA_idea_2 }
				remove_ideas = TUR_OPDA_idea_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_OPD_idea }
				remove_ideas = TUR_OPD_idea
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_OPD_idea_2 }
				remove_ideas = TUR_OPD_idea_2

	invest_in_ottoman_syria = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = { always = yes }
		target_trigger = { FROM = { tag = TUR } }
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_war_with = FROM
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TUR_state_to_be_invested
				var:ROOT.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = { NOT = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR } }
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FROM
				has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_syria
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_tt
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_mission = invest_in_ottoman_rumelia_mission }
					NOT = { has_mission = invest_in_ottoman_anatolia_mission }
					NOT = { has_mission = invest_in_ottoman_syria_mission } 
					NOT = { has_mission = invest_in_ottoman_mesapotamia_mission }
					NOT = { has_mission = invest_in_ottoman_trablusgarp_mission }
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 50
		fire_only_once = no
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				is_controlled_by = TUR
				OR = {
					state = 859
					state = 677
					state = 1023
					state = 852
					state = 554
					state = 553
					state = 858
					state = 454
					state = 856
					state = 455
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			TUR = {
				any_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						state = 859
						state = 677
						state = 1023
						state = 852
						state = 554
						state = 553
						state = 858
						state = 454
						state = 856
						state = 455
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_at_all }
		}
		complete_effect = {
			country_event = ottoman.42
			set_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans
			set_country_flag = investing_in_ottoman_syria
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.5
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories < 5
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 10
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 15
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 20
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 25
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_civilian_factories > 30
				add = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 25
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 50s
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = TUR
					value > 80
				}
				add = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = TUR
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_together_with = TUR
				add = 15
			}
			modifier = {
				tag = FRA
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 30
			}
			modifier = {
				tag = RUS
				add = -10
			}
		}
	}

				add = 100
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_pro_ottoman_rallies = {
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = TUR
				original_tag = ALB
			}
		}
		icon = GFX_decision_TUR_support_islamists
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 25
		days_remove = 15
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_pro_ottoman_rallies
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = TUR
							tag = ALB
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = TUR_pro_ottoman_rallies
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			ALB = {
				add_political_power = 75
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = escape_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_albanian_plot_plus_25_percents
			add_to_variable = {
				ALB_coup_detat = 25
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = fate_of_albania
					option = FATE_OF_ALBANIA_OTTOMAN_EMIRATE_OPTION
				}
				add = 100
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_ignite_albanian_coup = {
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = TUR
				original_tag = ALB
			}
		}
		icon = GFX_decision_TUR_islamic_revolts
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 0
		days_remove = 3
		available = {
			tag = ALB
			NOT = {
				has_decision = TUR_bring_ottoman_soldiers_to_vlore
				has_decision = TUR_obtain_landowners_support
				has_decision = TUR_setup_weapon_caches
				has_decision = TUR_pro_ottoman_rallies
			}
		}
		visible = { NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_ignite_albanian_coup } }
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = TUR
							tag = ALB
						}
					}
					ALB = {
						set_country_flag = TUR_ignite_albanian_coup
					}
					TUR = {
						set_country_flag = TUR_ignite_albanian_coup
					}
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						ALB_coup_detat < 0
					}
				}
				country_event = ww1_albania.33
				TUR = {
					country_event = ww1_albania.33
				}
				else = {
					random_list = {
						ALB_coup_detat = {
							country_event =  ww1_albania.32
							TUR = {
								country_event =  ww1_albania.32
							}
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = ww1_albania.33
							TUR = {
								country_event = ww1_albania.33
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				date > 1914.1.10
				add = 1000
			}
		}
	}
